Special Report by Tong Xingbai Jiang

The Problem of Knowledge and Action in the New Life Movement 282

(3)

— Recorded by Chen Dongbai

Second, the study of knowledge in the New Life Movement. Although the methods of the New Life are to be clean and simple in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, the purpose is to achieve righteousness, health, and shame. Therefore, the general public believes that to implement the New Life, one must first know etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Only by knowing etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame can one implement the New Life. This statement is common everywhere. Therefore, after the birth of the New Life Movement, the general public paid special attention to etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. However, I believe that although the New Life aims to achieve etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame cannot be separated from the life of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Therefore, as long as the life of clothing, food, housing, and transportation is disciplined, etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame can be expressed in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and it is not to do etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame outside of clothing, food, housing, and transportation.

Etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are abstract philosophies. In ancient times, many people were studying them, but opinions were divided and each had its own saying. So far, there is no final conclusion. It can be seen that the principles of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are not easy to understand. Guanzi said, "Etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four pillars of the country. If the four pillars are not strong, the country will decline and perish." Although Guanzi advocated etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame in this way, did he ever understand it himself? The Analects say, "The prince of the state plants a gate to block the door, and Guan also plants a forest to block the door. The prince of the state has a counter-slope for the good of the two princes, and Guan also has a counter-slope. If Guan Zhong knew propriety, he did not know propriety." It can be seen that Guan Zhong did not first understand the word propriety. The Biography of Guan Zhong in the Records of the Historian says that Guan Zhong and Shao Hu both served Gongzi Jiu. When Gongzi Jiu was killed by Duke Huan, Shao Hu died, but Guan Zhong did not die. Not only did he not die, but he also served Duke Huan of Qi. May I ask, did Guan Zhong know righteousness or not? Guan Zhong once partnered with Bao Shu to do business and shared profits, taking more for himself. May I ask, did Guan Zhong keep integrity or not? Guan Zhong once fought three battles and retreated three times without dying. In this way, did Guan Zhong know shame or not? According to the above, even Guan Zhong himself did not understand etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, not to mention other people. Therefore, we do not need to study the principles of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, because knowledge is difficult. Confucius said, "The people can be made to follow it, but not made to know it." He also said, "Those who know it are not as good as those who like it, and those who like it are not as good as those who enjoy it." This means that we do not need to understand it before we do it. Mr. Zhongshan also said, "Knowing is difficult." Seeking knowledge is certainly important, but it is the responsibility of those who are first to know and first to realize. Otherwise, "knowledge" will never be obtained and "action" will never be scheduled. Currently, everything in China wants to "know before acting." Although there is also meaning, it is impossible for everyone to be like this. Therefore, for the New Life, we do not necessarily have to "know before acting," that is, we do not need to study the principles of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, as long as we admit that etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are good morals and earnestly follow the New Life Covenant.

Third, the study of action in the New Life Movement. The New Life is entirely the way of life of the people of a country. As long as the people of a country have a certain disciplined way of life, this is the purpose of the country. In ancient China, etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame were emphasized, emphasizing action over knowledge. Those in power set an example and showed them the rules. Ordinary communities can all practice it, and society is very orderly. Even today, ordinary ignorant people and rural women still have this kind of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame in their treatment of people. In fact, they have completely become a habit, so it is naturally revealed. In terms of knowledge, they have never understood the principles of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. From this, it can be seen that the New Life Movement is not a question of knowledge at all, but a question of action. Just follow the New Life Covenant and you can express the spirit of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Mr. Zhongshan said, "Not knowing can also act" is to correct the Chinese people's problem of having to know before acting. Therefore, from now on, for the Life Movement, we do not need to seek its profound theory, just do it earnestly.

Fourth, conclusion. According to the above explanation of knowledge and action, summing up, we can get a conclusion that the New Life Movement is a question of action, not a question of knowledge. There is no need to seek its knowledge, but to seek its action. It does not matter whether we know it or not, but whether we act or not. Rather than wanting to know before acting, it is better to gain knowledge through action. (End)

Distant months saw long positions in the market raising prices one after another, and people's hearts remained good from beginning to end. Silk and Tea Cold Weather, Late Silkworm Season 304

The development of spring silkworms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is late. In places like Xiecun and Hushu near "Liangzhu", farmers who plant local varieties this year account for 40 to 50%. However, due to continuous spring rains and low temperatures, early silkworms have been found to have softening and microparticle diseases in the third sleep, resulting in a loss of 60 to 70%. Improved silkworm seeds have strong resistance and are still rarely damaged. They are now just waking up from their third sleep. In areas such as Xucun, Chang'an, and Xuxiang, although foreign silkworm seeds are affected by cold rain, they are still rarely damaged. The early batch has started to leaf out for the third sleep, and the late batch has just completed the second sleep. Local silkworm seeds eat more wet leaves in the third sleep, and the weather is too cold, causing them to spit black, leak yellow, and rot, resulting in 50 to 60% mortality. In "Fuyang", the amount of silkworm eggs raised in various cities and towns has decreased, and there are more farmers raising local varieties. The rural economy is bankrupt, and only families with mulberry trees are trying their best to raise them. However, the weather is not right, and there is more spring cold and rain. The local silkworms that need leaves during sleep all have silkworm diseases and lose a lot of leaves. Improved silkworm seeds develop later, and are currently only completing their second sleep. Farmers in various cities and towns of "Liyang" have little interest in raising silkworms due to losses in previous years. Instructors have gone to various villages to distribute improved seeds and encourage people to raise them. During the incubation period, the weather was cold, and the ants only hatched after 14 or 15 days. They are now only opening leaves for the first sleep. Only 60% of the local silkworm seeds have hatched, and all types of silkworms cannot hatch, it is said.

The silk production is limited, and the demand exceeds the supply. Last month, the British ship loaded 28 packages to India.

Record of the Pervasive Fragrance 307

— Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Therefore, the position of this director is absolutely unworthy for Meng Fuxiang. He is simply a completely useless puppet. Please pay attention to the following, and you can believe it. Because the Empress Dowager was eager to know some knowledge about trains, she sent someone to summon Meng Fuxiang. When he came, he naturally kowtowed respectfully first. After kowtowing, although he stood up, he did not dare to look up. His eyes were always looking at the floor, waiting for the Empress Dowager to inquire.

"What exactly makes this train move?" The Empress Dowager's first question.

"Replying to the Empress Dowager... Replying to the Old Buddha," Meng Fuxiang had a stutter, so his speech was very slow and disconnected. "It is these workers on the train who drive the train!"

"Is this still afraid that I don't know it! Now, I just ask you, how exactly do they

drive the train?"

"This servant deserves to die! This... this servant doesn't know! This servant doesn't know! This servant dares not... dares not... dare not reply rashly!"

"Remember at the previous station," Although his reply was so disappointing, the Empress Dowager insisted on asking him. "For what reason did our train once retreat to the back? Now tell me, why can these wheels roll forward?"

"This... this... servant kno... kno... knows! Replying to the Empress Dowager! This is done by the driver!"

"Then, how do they stop this train?" "Replying to the Empress Dowager! Six people jump off the train and run to the last car to grab the wheel. As long as they grab it with all their strength, the train will stop!"

This answer may be more accurate than Meng Fuxiang himself thought, because he always thought that the brakemen must have forcibly pulled the train. (25)

Flowers in the Field 308

— Qing Qu

When you go to the suburbs and look around, between the ridges and fields, there are splendid golden flowers, and they bloom densely, as if drawing squares. If you are flying in an airplane in the sky and look down at the lower world, don't say that the round earth is a turbid and dark Asura field. In reality, it has turned into a golden world, reflecting into its eyes. There are also small flowers like butterflies, fluttering in the spring breeze, as if flying after each other. Especially the color is white with purple, and the purple has very large black spots, so from a distance, it looks like countless butterflies gathered in the lush green grass. These two kinds of flowers are not wild, but agricultural crops in the field.

The first kind: is the flower of rapeseed, which is said to have been obtained from outside the Great Wall. The place of production is called "Yuntai Garrison". Therefore, this kind of flower is also called "Yun Tai Flower". The petals are cruciform, with one pistil and six stamens. At the bottom of the stamens, there is also a green small ball, which scientists call the nectar gland, which constantly secretes sweet juice. Therefore, many bees

constantly shuttle back and forth, and are extremely close to the rapeseed flowers, as if forming an indissoluble bond. Farmers sow this kind of vegetable in winter, and in spring they harvest its stalk, commonly called "vegetable sword", which can also be made into kimchi and stored in jars. Shanghai also calls it "Taiwan Heart Vegetable", which is actually rapeseed. Its seeds can be pressed for oil, an indispensable auxiliary product for making biscuits.

The second kind: is the flower of broad beans, which bloom in August of last year and have to plant seeds. It was not until the sericulture season this year that they bloomed, so the fruits they bear are called "silkworm beans." Its stem is like a ridge, the pod is long and wide, and the bean is flat and large, about half an inch in size. When it is hard and old, the color turns green, and there is a black bay on the head, like an eyebrow, so some people say: the term "silkworm bean" comes from this. This thing can be eaten as a vegetable or made into sauce, and its sales are extremely wide. If the harvest is abundant, farmers compete to call it "small ripe." Yang Wanli, a former Shanghainese poet, said: "Emerald pods are lined with light green beads, sweet fraud cliff is dense and soft fraud su, sand bottles are newly ripe with West Lake water, lacquer pots are shared with dawn dew, taste and cherry plum are three beneficial friends, the name is due to silkworm cocoons and a thread of brilliance, the old farmer's troupe is learning together, and the score is written in the poem as a farming book." This poem is an extremely wonderful work about broad beans.

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Eighth: Coincidence: Shared Viewing;痴 情: Picking up a Handkerchief; Inquisitive: Two Times Asking About Illness; Mistake: Improperly Delivering a Letter

But he seemed unwilling to move his seat or walk away, considering his past relationship with her. As a result, the anxiety in his heart was all reflected on his face, turning red from his cheeks, straight to the back of his ears. However, Ji Zhi still did not feel it, and kept sniffing towards this side for the source of the fragrance. Finally, he still found the fragrance, which turned out to be from the wool scarf. Sketches of Fallen Flowers 310

— Huoxueming

The brilliant sunshine and hazy scenery have passed the season of yellow plums, and in the silvery sound of rain, it quietly flies away. On the muddy cultivated embankment, there are scattered peach blossoms, and in the gloomy wet sky, there are light catkins.

Above the Luo valley-like flowing waves, drooping with turning green willow silk. Alas! The crisp-boned sunny spring of Jiangnan is far gone.

Sitting in a small study room with shrimp whisker curtains blocking the sun, burning a cigarette, quietly looking at the clear blue sky, a fallen flower skimmed past, being kicked by a swallow: together they fell to the eaves, so I rolled up the curtain, wanting to catch the wandering spring-is it a good phenomenon?

The soul, unexpectedly, had fallen into a backwater under the water pavilion, swallowed into the belly by a swimming fish, regurgitated again, blown into the waves, that spring soul was much thinner!

If in front of you is a clear lake, and outside the lake is a bamboo forest, the drizzle is falling delicately, and the fallen flowers are also falling: following the silk wind to send to the resting window lattice, bringing a little lonely residual fragrance: at the same time, several water birds also fly shoulder to shoulder with the fallen flowers, these shadows are all projected onto the lake surface, that is truly a music without any sound!

If it is a clear night with a new moon, the moon shadow is blown onto the railing by the wind, and the pear flowers in the courtyard are falling dimly, as light as snowflakes, as dense as silver rain; yet there is no hint of sadness.

If you return after fishing a few small fish, driving a short boat, rowing with the oar, and parting the evening mist covering the lake, a fallen flower blows obliquely from the shore, blowing onto my smoke hat. The hat is woven from green bamboo and cannot bear it, so it slips down the vast water mist, like the spirit of a fairy, smiling charmingly at people.

Fallen flowers have a gentle and graceful posture, a洒脱神韵洒脱 神韵潇洒 divine charm, and a light and agile dream. Fallen flowers symbolize the yearning of poets and girls.

Watching the Lantern Procession in Chang'an 312

— Wu Xiaochen

This time the author went from Pinghu to

Chongde, riding in

a car. Originally, he could have arrived on the same day, but unfortunately, the

car from Hai Ning to Chang'an broke down

and delayed my journey. Later, I changed to a steamship, and when I arrived in Chang'an, it was already dark. The boat connecting to Chongde had long disappeared without a trace, but Chang'an was holding a grand lantern procession. I happened to arrive at the right time, so I stayed overnight in Chang'an. The lantern procession is very popular in the western part of Zhejiang, and it can be said to be a kind of entertainment for the common people. The authorities were afraid of affecting social order, so they had stopped it for more than ten years. Recently, various places have felt the economic recession, so they thought of welcoming the lanterns again, or it could revitalize the market. Xiashi, Haining, Chongde, Jiaxing, Zhouwangmiao and other places will be held one after another, and Chang'an is just opening the end. The Chang'an lantern procession starts on the 17th and lasts for four days. There are a total of sixteen platforms, which are divided into sixteen groups and united together to welcome. Each has its own lanterns and its own characteristics. It starts at 7 pm and will welcome the lanterns until 2 am. Among them, the Pinfangtai building tower is full of electric lights on the tower, which light up for a while and go out for a while, which is most appreciated. There is also a group of Qixi pictures, with accompaniment of fine music in front, and the melody is moderate. It is still quite pleasant to listen to. Other things such as lions,涼亭麒凉亭麒lions, pavilions, unicorns, etc., are connected together, which is very long. Of course, there are many viewers who express welcome. There are also not a few who feel that this kind of lantern is too vulgar. There is also a kind of slogan on the lamp, which can be said to express the thoughts of a part of the common people. The slogans are "Silkworm flowers are luxuriant", "Celebrate the rising peace together", "Enjoy with the people", and "Four seasons of peace".

All hotels and restaurants took the opportunity to raise prices and make a fortune. The single guest room that originally sold for 4 jiao was raised to 1.2 yuan. The price of side dishes also doubled compared to usual. The reason they raised prices was that the hotels and restaurants bore a lot of expenses for this lantern procession. Therefore, they had no choice but to think about the tourists.

Wuxi Flower Garden 313

— Yin Qiu

The weather is clear and sunny, the spring scenery is brilliant, and Suzhou and Hangzhou, known as paradise, have become the focus of travelers, feeling exceptionally lively. This time, I and a few friends agreed to travel to Wuxi, planning to spend a full day and return to Suzhou on the same day. Once the agreement was set, we took a special express train at nine in the morning. After the train started, we saw the shadow of Tiger Hill Pagoda, towering into the blue sky, as if waving goodbye to us. Gradually it became farther and smaller, quite charming. Soon, we were immersed in the rural scenery, as if walking through a painting. Before long, we could see Xishan in the distance, and saw factory chimneys, as dense as a lush forest, showing the prosperity of industry.

Because we had to visit Meiyuan first, we took a streetcar to Yinglong Bridge, then changed to a car, and went directly to the garden gate. The garden is located in Dongshan, west of Kaiyuan Road. It was rebuilt by the industrialist Rong Desheng on the site of the peach orchard of Xu Dianyi, a Jinshi in the Qing Dynasty, and planted extensively with plum trees, hence its current name. Entering the gate, you immediately see a huge stone, engraved with the two characters "Meiyuan." As the road gradually advances, the ground gradually rises, and through the winding flowers and trees, passing Xixin Pavilion, you can climb to Tianxing Terrace and see Taihu Lake. Further up is Xiangxue Xuan, where one can sit and recite poetry, and around it is Liuyue Village and Little Luofu, facing the ultimate peak of the mountains. The mountain scenery and lake light are open and lovely, and the sails going up and down are especially magnificent. Thus, a poem was born: "Leaning against the clear sky at the high point of Meiyuan, the mountain scenery and lake light are all in sight, most of all the sails are infinitely beautiful, natural poetic material that is difficult to paint."

Halfway up the mountain is the Taihu Hotel, providing meals for guests. Because it was past noon, we rested in the hotel, gathered around a round table. Although the dishes were not excellent, our appetites were better than usual. After a full meal, we went down the mountain and out of the garden, and took a car to Little Ji Mountain. The mountain is west of Little Penglai, surrounded by water on three sides. In summer, it is known for its lotus flowers, making it a popular summer resort. Unfortunately, the architecture mostly adopts European styles, failing to avoid vulgarity. Looking from afar at Yuantouzhu, the green trees are lush and shady, and the yellow walls are faintly visible. There is a small ferry available, but because the wind suddenly picked up and the waves were extremely large, and we also had to tour..., we did not go. Another poem was born: "Driving straight up Little Ji Mountain, a corner of a pavilion beside the water bay, pointing remotely at the famous scenic spot of Yuantouzhu, the good wind sends back the sound of the waves."

The garden is located on the edge of Five Mile Lake, and was the villa of Wang Yuqing, a Wuxi native. We took a car to go there, and the journey was extremely long. Once there, there were Thousand-Step Cloister, Hanbi Pavilion, Lakeside Thatched Cottage, and other scenic spots. The red railings and green balustrades are exquisitely structured, and the Stone Embankment, Snow Wave, and other mountains are arranged like screens. Along the embankment by the lake, the willow branches spread green and the flower buds stretch red, resembling the edge of West Lake. Between looking up and down, I continued to get a poem: "The scenery by Five Mile Lake is clear, the Su Garden willows are dark and the flowers are bright, the thousand-step cloister has three overlapping peaks, stirring my leisurely, otherworldly emotions."

Free Talk

Village Gleanings (3) 314

— Feng Zi

(3) Village Education

Generally speaking, everyone has some unique quirks, or perhaps what is called personality! In life, there are things that one absolutely will not do, things that one must do, things that are optional, and things that are better done this way than that way. Belonging to the latter, I have a very obvious quirk, which is that I would rather listen to an old woman chanting the Amitabha Sutra than talk about world affairs with a village pedant.

World affairs are inherently difficult to talk about, but if you talk about them with a village pedant, there is even more suffering of "unspeakable." Every time I return to my hometown, apart from looking at the farmers' operations and talking with the elders about the village situation, I rarely interact with these people.

But the "good words and deeds" of the pedants will certainly not be "buried and unknown" because of my non-interaction.

In our village, there is only half a person who can be called a pedant, and that is the teacher hired from another county for the village school. The reason why I say half is not only because he is not from the village, but also because he does not have the talent of a pedant, but has the views of a pedant; he does not have the lofty detachment of a pedant, but has the arrogance of a pedant; he must occupy the upper seat at banquets, and when he sees the school directors, he bows and stands like a servant, his pedantic and sour demeanor is all too obvious. When teaching, his pronunciation and meaning are so vague that even a few elementary school students cannot cope with it.

But he is still able to continue teaching.

There are a total of seventy or so students in this school, and there are two teachers. The other one is nominally the principal, but what he manages is village affairs, not school affairs. He is busy being the secretary of the school directors, the strategist of the village head, and a guest on the seats of the gentry. He entrusts the seventy or so young students to our pedant as if entrusting orphans.

The motivation of the gentry to establish this school, is definitely not to promote education, but to save face for the village. To put it more clearly, it is to save face for themselves. This is not an initiative of a few gentlemen in a small village. I don't know how many gentlemen in the country are running educational undertakings to save face. This kind of behavior of seeking fame is originally not worthy of deep blame. But believing in these two treasures and neglecting children's education to such an extent is really unforgivable.

I inquired in several nearby villages and felt that their casual attitude towards children's education was really shocking. The private school system has passed, but the poison that presided over the private schools is still able to shake in the new school system. This is really a problem that urgently needs attention in the countryside. National affairs can be temporarily ignored.

○○○○

Petty Cleverness and Great Wisdom 315

— Ne

Great people generally have a certain understanding of life and the universe. No matter how talented a person is, they cannot reach this level without a very long period of experience, thinking, and learning. The achievements of scholars in the East and West are mostly after middle age, and that is why.

After having a solid understanding of many things, then in the course of life, there is a certain direction. Direction is not obtained by chance (except for buying lottery tickets, things in the world are rarely accidental). For example, gambling, there is also one's own intention in it. Usually, it requires careful investigation, rich experience, and decisive judgment -- in other words, it requires great wisdom.

Great wisdom is not necessarily innate, but is formed from acquired learning. And this

often requires going through some pain. The scholars who sought the Tao in ancient times, just looking at the Song Confucians, know how much hard work was spent. Or they went from the military strategists to the Buddhist family, and then from the Buddhist family back to the Confucian family; or they thought without eating or sleeping, and finally "investigated" bamboo but never understood it, and instead made themselves sick. These kinds of things seem so ridiculous to us modern people, but the efforts that the predecessors spent, taking a path that did not lead anywhere, and standing back at the crossroads to prove "this road does not work," saves later generations a lot of effort, and is still great.

But petty cleverness is different. This can be said to be "small talent." The difference between small and great is like the difference between pine and cypress and shallow grass, and the difference between rivers and seas and puddles; the difference between cleverness and wisdom is like someone who looks like a saint but is expelled by Zeng Zi; a kite can be made into an airplane, but it cannot carry people.

Unfortunately, the people of our country today are all heading towards the path of petty cleverness. There are many scholars in Jiangnan, and once they step into the fork in the road of petty cleverness, there is no cure. There are fewer scholars in the north, but there is less of the atmosphere of petty cleverness. When a scholar is produced, he is a very great scholar.

The tendency of cleverness is to be quick-witted, delicate, lightweight, sparse, unwilling to work hard, and content with the status quo. These are all causes of decline and omens of destruction. Look at the figures of today, especially the "literati," who is not drifting here and there with a little bit of petty cleverness?

The Night of the City 316

— Zang Kejia

Covered with a network of red silk,

a pair of excited eyes wide open,

like a woman defiled ten thousand times, swollen eyelids unable to hold calm. No charming stars can be found in the sky, unable to point to the Big Dipper to determine the seasons, unable to distinguish the silence of the vast Milky Way, unable to see the rosy clouds embracing the moon: countless lights exchange in mid-air, like countless hearts beating to the extreme. Hellfire burns on the ground, a large, chaotic shadow running for life, heels seeming to fear getting stained with flames. Fire dragons streak across the ground, with a bit of a frantic roar; dappled tigers rush around, shining a pair of terrifying eyes; eight hooves rush forward desperately, unable to care for the peace of a balanced carriage; rickshaws are the most clumsy and pitiful, like an ant dragging a mantis, a piece of floating music enclosing the city, a demon using polyphony to proclaim evil. Such an ancient taste, unable to tell its dreams: dogs barking at spring stars in the deep alleys, a cock crowing at dawn, light dreams lingering around the dying lamp, the sound of the night spun out on the spinning wheel. The colorful lights in the venue shine dizzily, illuminating the fluttering robes of the immortals, the singing floats and sinks with drunken hearts, who still thinks this is in the night? The factory machines turn human hearts, also holding joy, the grinding sound, shaking people's souls like raindrops hitting duckweed, staggering in a daze, this city night is really worth praising, it is both hell and heaven, it is still generous and impartial,

overflowing with clear songs, and not covering up the suffocating breath, really want it to have a happy explosion,

to find some peace in the ashes.

"Han Hai" 318

— Shu

"Han Hai," twelve volumes, edited by Shen Xihou and appraised by his teacher Chen Meigong, collects more than a thousand letters from the Zhou case to the Ming Dynasty, with Ming letters accounting for four-fifths. It is a Ming edition. Its compilation uses a classification method, separately divided into twelve parts: emotion, beautiful words, self-narration, interpersonal affection, medicine, anger, leisure, reclining travel, literature, statecraft, and good words, each part with several types. The selection criteria, according to the example words, say that "vulgar and corrupt words in the letters are not worth bothering the subordinates, and should be erased by hand. As for the bones being icy and the red clouds reflecting the sun, those that move people's hearts should be collected immediately." However, although the selection is excellent, it is still inevitable to have one or two shortcomings, that is, occasionally the selected person's travel notes, essays, etc. are also included as letters, and the author's famous... are inconsistent. For example, Hongdao is sometimes called Yuan Hong, sometimes Yuan Shigong, and sometimes Yuan Zhonglang. I cannot agree with these two points.

The book has a preface written by Chen Meigong on "the first day of the fourth month of the Gengwu year of Chongzhen." Its main points are, first of all, pointing out that the letter item, after Yang Yongxiu and Wang Shizhen's "Qingcai" came out, "there was no life." The so-called "lifelike" letters should be like "flying waterfalls hanging down, chaotic cliffs covered with the moon," "clear water as silk, recruiting cool beads, coming from places that people have not reached," "bright as a hundred houses," "witty words piercing the heart, obliterating sentences that are not painful or itchy." The selectors of "Han Hai" possess these conditions, so he "swims in the sea and picks it up." Secondly, he probably felt that letters and essays were not valued by the world, and said with emotion, "Tao Shihang used bamboo heads and wood scraps, to make a living: writing is neither big nor small. If there is a true spirit reflected on the paper, it is wisdom." In the final paragraph, he expresses his feelings about current affairs, saying, "Now that the beacon fires are about to be extinguished and the Rong rope is self-determined, composing poems is not a strategy, and the eight-legged essay is useless; I will think of a piece of paper from the Han Dynasty, which is better than ten thousand troops, and Emperor Guangwu of the Han Dynasty's clear vision of thousands of miles is more than just playing with double fish." The introduction is not much, but Meigong's understanding of letters, his recognition of essays, and the era's bitterness hidden in his heart are all seen here. It is an important article by Meigong and a powerful document in the literary movement at the time, which we cannot lightly let go.

then, "Once you play with essays, it's better than reading ten thousand books," and the future will naturally be optimistic and "the world will be peaceful."

Mr. Xu Maoyong's opinions in "Novel and Essay" are not much different from what I have seen. I said that essays and essays are products of the aristocracy or the scholar-official class in terms of the origin of the style (Origin). Mr. Xu Maoyong is discussing the current situation. As for reportage literature, although its nature is similar to essays and feuilletons, is it the same in genre? Must be considered. The two are products of different social foundations. This article is not a disagreement with what Mr. Xu Maoyong said. Because someone is arguing against what Mr. Xu Maoyong and I have said, so I wrote this article again.

A Glimpse of Bansong Garden 319

— Hei Ying

I like to read travel notes, and I often tell people about the benefits of travel: but in fact, I am not a very enthusiastic traveler. I have been in Shanghai for almost two years, and there are many places that I feel I should have visited but have not. Living in the city from morning to night every day, breathing in coal smoke, and listening to the noise of machines, I finally feel a bit disgusted.

Taking advantage of the clear spring weather, I invited Lin and Lingling, and with a dry heart, went to Bansong Garden in Nanshi. When the car drove to Nanshi, Lingling said:

"This is Chinese territory."

Having lived in the quiet countryside at first, and then spending every day under the skyscrapers of the concession, seeing the cobblestone roads and small, old shops here, it was as if I had come to an ancient town. I wanted to recite a seven-character poem or a ci poem, but the car was bumping so badly: Lingling's body almost fell into my arms. Arriving at the entrance of Bansong Garden, it was a little after two in the afternoon. Lin bought our tickets, and we walked through the gate together, walking on a corridor.

Neither Lin nor I had been here before; this time we had to let the enthusiastic Lingling lead the way. I looked at her slender figure, thinking that her young, innocent heart must be very happy. We had only known each other recently; because of a small language barrier, I had not said many words to her. But, just now I had said these words:

"Lingling! I want to learn Shanghainese."

Yes, when I could speak Shanghainese, I could be friends with Lingling; aren't there many words hidden in our hearts that we can't say?

There were many antiques on display here for sale, and looking at the prices, they were not very high: it's just that I didn't feel any interest in these things at all. I am, after all, a city person, and although I feel bitter after breathing in coal smoke, I am also unfamiliar with mountains and water!

On a man-made river, there were small boats rowing; a warm breeze blew, and a smile appeared on Lingling's face. The water was green, and the reeds on both sides were also green. On the artificial mountain, a tourist wearing a melon-skin cap was singing "Wujiapo" loudly; on the bridge, a group of female students were folding photos.

"Let's take one too."

After hearing Lin's words, Lingling jumped to the lake. Many people were leisurely sitting in the pavilion drinking tea: I don't understand the pleasure of drinking tea very much, so I hurriedly went back to the river to row a boat.

A group of donkeys were running and braying over there, with women who looked like concubines riding on their backs.

There was also a gambling-like game field here, which reminded me of the second day after I first came to Shanghai, and what I saw in the Great World was also like this. Lin planned to spend a dime or two for Lingling to play something, but the result was that she didn't get anything!

In an instant, it was already dusk and twilight.

The quaint Bansong Garden could not keep me. Just like the beautiful West Lake made me feel lonely. Finally, I got back into the car, letting it drive at a speed of sixty degrees, rushing from the cobblestone road straight to the skyscrapers.

Shanpu Lottery Tang 320

— Xi Ru

Afa finally made up his mind. He would try it no matter what.

He had made such a determination hundreds of times today, but every time he touched the money in his pocket, he would cancel out this courage. The money jingling in his pocket was a dollar and a few cents. And this dollar and a few cents had hundreds of uses, each of which was necessary and urgent.

There was no way, what could this money be used for? It was better not to use it at all, so as not to seem to look down on other uses. "If I win! Wouldn't that be...?"

He wasn't a fool, he understood that if he suddenly hit the jackpot, he would have a way to add hundreds more uses. Who could say that he, Afa, wouldn't have this luck?! Wasn't it just the other day when he was drinking tea at Good Food Restaurant that he heard people saying that the last first prize was won by a dock coolie?

Now it seemed that even the heavens would sometimes bless the poor.

He kept comforting and defending himself like this. He had already quickly turned from... shell to Kuaifu Street.

He knew the biggest lottery shop in the vicinity, called Xinglong Lottery Shop.

Two ground-based lamps, like door gods, stood opposite each other on both sides of the door.

The lanterns were as thick as two people could hug, a foot and a half long, the dim red candlelight hidden in the oil paper shell, like a pair of cunning eyes flashing. Pasted on the lantern shell were four red characters that were thick and flat, like several fat crabs stacked together: National Defense Expenses.

Afa walked to the door, hesitated for a moment, and immediately walked straight past it. What if he ran into someone he knew? They would definitely laugh at him in front of his face: Look at Afa, that poor wretch, trying to get rich quick! Hmph! Really, a toad wanting to eat swan meat! Hmph! No, no, he couldn't compare to the rich, who spent two dimes as casually as if they were spending a copper coin. He had to use these few dollars and cents until he found work again. There were so many people from the countryside coming to the city to look for work, just a casual glance on the street corner and there were dozens of them, squatting, standing, wandering, waiting for work, no, no, he had to save and use frugally, don't be so absurd!·····

He walked straight to Yidinghao Tea House. A burst of urgent string music rose from the third floor, and a female's sharp voice followed, beginning to sing. It was then that he realized that he had already passed twenty or thirty shops.

"What do you do? Go back or not go back and try it?" His heart was asking him. He hesitated. If he didn't try it, then wouldn't the determination of the last few times be in vain? Not trying meant that everything was unresolved, there was no hope, and he would be poor for the rest of his life! Also, maybe this time he would really win the first prize? If he didn't buy it and let the good luck slip away in his hands for nothing, wouldn't that be a wrongful death?! Anyway, he was poor, what did two dimes matter... He turned back again.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

International Situation 321

— Gu She

Many people predicted that 1936 would be the outbreak period of the Second World War. Judging from the current situation, the realization of this prediction does have some possibility. The facts have already been revealed in this way: in Europe, disarmament has long reached a dead end, and the conflict between Germany and France, and between France and Italy, is becoming more acute day by day. Britain's policy of maintaining the European balance of power is currently useless. At the same time, in the Far East, there is the opposition between Japan and the United States, and between Britain and Japan. The unlimited expansion of Japanese imperialism has almost brought this opposition to a fever pitch, and the opposition between Japan and the Soviet Union

further complicates this problem. In this way, the eastern and western hemispheres are simultaneously shrouded in war clouds. We only see the diplomats of various countries, how they are strategizing and arranging this war situation. At the same time, the armaments factories of various countries are stepping up the manufacture of munitions. At present, it has indeed reached the point where "the mountain rain is about to come and the wind fills the building." The international situation is becoming tighter day by day, already forecasting that the god of the Second World War will soon descend on the world.

The struggle between France and Germany has long been the whole of the central issue of Europe, and with the addition of the struggle between France and Italy, this situation has become even more complicated. Hitler came to power, and the German regime, with the landlord bourgeoisie as its background, desperately needed to expand its economic hegemony abroad; France was its only fighter. What the French capitalists needed was to permanently grasp the monopoly situation on the European continent, so that all countries in Europe would be subject to their control. The rise of Germany was of course something they could never allow. In this way, the struggle between Germany and France was played out in an even more fierce situation than the Anglo-German struggle before the war. The struggle between France and Italy further transformed this European struggle situation into a triangular form, and intricately caused more complex effects. What Britain demanded was to consistently maintain the European balance of power, unite the forces of Europe, and deal with the United States. Unfortunately, this policy has also reached a dead end. How can this European struggle situation be relatively harmonized? This is what Britain is currently painstakingly planning to deal with. However, the objective facts show the opposite situation. The complete failure of disarmament, which can no longer be reversed, clearly indicates to people that the disputes in Europe can only be resolved through war.

Looking at the Far East again. The opposition between Japan and the United States is something everyone knows. The degree of opposition between Britain and Japan is no less than that of the United States. Japan's September 18th Incident had already opened the prelude to the Second World War, but at that time, various countries were burying themselves in preparations, so although Japan launched first, it would not immediately come into contact. Recently, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs unofficially issued a statement that China must be exclusively dominated by Japan, and other countries are not allowed to interfere. This situation has entered a new stage. What remains a problem now is that there is still no tinder to ignite the fire. Once the tinder is obtained, the outbreak of war will be tomorrow's affair.

The Far East and Europe are simultaneously opening the prelude to the Second World War. The outbreak period is approaching day by day. At present, all that remains is for the war deployments of various countries to be completed, and then the bloody killing business will begin. Regardless of whether the period is in 1936, the world will inevitably go through an even more cruel massacre. And the present is the period of intensifying preparations.

When imperialism develops to its peak, there must be a war. Only war is its final way out. However, the opposite of war is decline. Regardless of whether it is willing, history will inevitably evolve in this way. Imperialism often makes itself its own gravedigger.

What about the Chinese people standing in this war crisis? China is now the target of their struggles. How to fight our way out of this war crisis is what we should be preparing for at present!

A Treasure of the Three Eastern Provinces! Ginseng! 322

— Yangyang

Recently, news reports stated that the Japanese were harvesting ginseng in Jilin and had already transported large quantities into the mainland for sale. They have established management offices in Tianjin and Beijing, with a large organization, and are prohibiting people from the northern country from harvesting, which is truly heartbreaking! Whether or not land rights exist, we won't discuss, because the lost land of the Northeast has long ceased to belong to us. However, those who have always relied on ginseng harvesting for their livelihoods are now unemployed, and there is no prospect of a solution. It is a truly hopeless situation. As the old saying goes, "Better to be a dog in peaceful times than a person in chaotic times." Now, it can be changed to "Better to be a dog in a strong country than a person in a weak country." It is useless to bring up sad things, and pointless to talk about them. Let's talk about ginseng instead. I remember a northeastern saying: "The Three Eastern Provinces have three treasures: ginseng, deer antler, and Ula grass." In fact, the treasures of the three provinces are not limited to these. Apart from the natural development of mineral resources, there are also some treasures that are not directly related to the wealthy, so they are not valued by the world. Ginseng grows in the old mountains of Jilin, deep in the forests, but it must not be shaded by trees, and must be in a place where sunlight can reach it to grow. It is considered a perennial herbaceous plant, but in the history of Chinese medicine, it occupies one of the top three positions. Its uses are most closely related to the wealthy. In other words, it can cure almost any ailment suffered by the wealthy. It can treat all kinds of deficiencies, is warming without being drying, and nourishing without being heating. The slogans about its efficacy can all strike a chord in the hearts of the wealthy. But the poor have absolutely no connection with it. Even passing by a butcher shop, they cannot feast on it, but can only swallow saliva and sigh in vain. Just look at the ginseng shops facing each other in the second alley of Langfangtou in Beijing, their grandeur is no less than the remittance shops and silver houses of the past!

Ginseng is most valuable when it reaches fifty or sixty years old. Its "biography" can be roughly divided into six stages: one to five years, it grows one "掌子" (zhang zi, palm-like leaf); five to ten years, it grows two leaves, called "二來子" (er lai zi, two-coming leaf); twenty years, it grows three leaves, called "三台子" (san tai zi, three-platform leaf); thirty years, it grows four leaves, called "四品葉" (si pin ye, four-rank leaf); from thirty to forty, to fifty, and to sixty years, it goes through the names of "五品葉" (wu pin ye, five-rank leaf) and "六品葉" (liu pin ye, six-rank leaf), and naturally grows all six leaves. If the roots in the soil, the head, tail, and mother branches are complete, it may not be possible to buy one even for several hundred taels of silver. Most of the ginseng harvesters are from within the Guan (mountain passes), mostly from Henan and Shanxi provinces. They form groups of twenty people each. Before entering the mountains, assignments are determined, and they carry weapons to guard against robbers and wild beasts, like explorers. Those walking in a straight line keep a distance of over a hundred paces between each person in the group, calling out to each other to avoid getting lost. If one of them sees ginseng sprouts, they shout "棒棰" (bang chui, club/ginseng), and the companions behind ask, "What 棒棰?" The one who discovered the ginseng sprouts observes its appearance to determine what kind it is, and replies with "某棒棰" (a certain club/ginseng). At this time, everyone swarms forward, unanimously shouting, "拏!" (na, grab!). The procedure involves tying the ginseng sprouts with red thread, laying out oilcloth, and digging carefully around it while lying down, using a bamboo knife. The roots and whiskers must not be damaged in the slightest. If it cannot be completed in one or two days, they stay and guard it, waiting for the entire ginseng to be extracted. Then, they present offerings and kowtow to thank the mountain god. If the harvest is a large six-leaf ginseng, a whole sheep must be used as a sacrificial offering. Now that the Japanese have monopolized and control everything, not allowing Chinese people to participate, it is not known how they are digging ginseng. It is said that the matter of harvesting ginseng does indeed contain a semi-mysterious meaning!

Watching the Fun 323

— Juefu

Watching the fun is originally something our Chinese people value. Under a lonely lamp, watching people box, wrestle, and fight is certainly interesting; but a small quarrel between a couple of people on the street will often attract a group of passersby to surround and stare intently.

However, this only refers to things that can be directly seen within our line of sight. In addition, like hearing someone tell a bloody story, or seeing in magazines and newspapers that some people have been killed somewhere, or that some celebrity has caused some great disaster, it is also strangely interesting and fascinating.

If someone were to ask why people have this kind of psychology, I believe that it is probably because most people's hearts are too empty and too lonely. What they need is intense stimulation, like watching movies of lions and tigers fighting, or figure skaters dancing on ice.

Because this is the general psychology of modern society, a group of people who run magazines and newspapers, seeing this point, specialize in creating shocking news, or secretly attacking and slandering others, to please the readers. Moreover, some people among colleagues mark out different flags, attacking and scolding each other. From the lines of text, it seems as if they must fight to the death. But behind the scenes, they are shaking hands and laughing: "We are victorious!"

Originally, liking to watch the fun is not a very bad thing. If one can distinguish right from wrong and be inspired by it, joining the group of those who are making the excitement, becoming one of them, one would not be ridiculed as being like loose sand, or a cold-blooded animal. However, the people of our land of propriety and righteousness deeply understand the doctrine of the mean. Watching the fun is just watching. There is no expression when watching, and afterwards, it is forgotten as if nothing had happened.

In recent years, exciting things have emerged endlessly in our China. This is truly a great blessing bestowed by Heaven upon our people who love excitement!

On Being Jilted 324

— Jun

There is being jilted only when there is love. It's just that this is a pastime for leisurely young masters and ladies to spend their lives with eating and drinking. Poor bachelors rarely have this blessing. It is precisely because life is so leisurely that the days feel like years. They can only waste all their time completely on love, and they think that it is more important than any legitimate career. Love and life are almost becoming a two-in-one relationship. Without love, they simply cannot live, and if they unfortunately encounter heartbreak, then they are even more unable to live. This is especially true for the men. Once they are heartbroken, they are like soulless beings. This is not right, that is not right, causing them to eat without tasting, sleep restlessly, sighing all day long, the state of misery like losing their parents. Some even want to live and die because of this, feeling that since they are already heartbroken, everything is empty, and all thoughts are dashed. Life has no more meaning or value, so they bravely take sleeping pills, hang themselves, jump into the sea... they must destroy their lives. In fact, this kind of behavior seems a little "that" to me, and it is not considered clever. Or perhaps there are some with Ah Q-like spirits. Of course, I am not opposed to the men indulging in love, and I don't want to speak like a moral gentleman, saying don't take love so seriously and should do some meaningful things. It is true that love is an indispensable thing in life, but I think there is no need to be too serious, especially about being jilted. Being too serious is just asking for trouble, and pain is deserved, self-inflicted, and who can pity you? So being casual not only doesn't cause pain, but also takes advantage of happiness. Moreover, in this materialistic metropolis, love is gilded, full of the stench of money. As long as you have endless money, then I guarantee that you will be successful everywhere. All ethereal spirits are ghosts' talk. At the same time, women have become commodities, with a certain price, and they will pay you a certain quality of goods. Of course, there are also differences between miscellaneous sales and wholesale. But in general, it cannot escape the nature of buying and selling. Urban women mostly have a romantic character, despising chastity and integrity by thirteen points, and being fascinated by so-called free love. They have not gotten the benefits, but they have everything bad, liking novelty, stimulation, and activity. Today this one, tomorrow that one, in any case, there is no lasting interest, playing with love like a child's play. This is all a common prototype of fashionable girls currently in vogue.

The Trend of Aesthetic Attitude: Idealism 325

— Wenguang

At the beginning of the year, some things changed, some turned left, some turned right; it seems that if they don't turn a bit, they are not suitable for survival.

Perhaps some people say, "Everything can change, but people's aesthetic attitude will always find young girls or young boys beautiful, and not old women or old men with wrinkled skin and white hair, right?"

Now, let's not be too assertive. Facts are the most eloquent. First, let's observe how people's aesthetic attitudes have been trending recently.

In 1934, twelve thousand superstars participated in the Miss America election. The queen elected was May Wray, who was over sixty years old. The runner-up was Will Rogers, who was an old man. American men, who used to be fascinated by gentlemen and legs, have also changed their love. Their focus on aesthetics has shifted to paying attention to the performance skills and artistic contributions of the stars, discarding that materialistic aesthetic attitude. Otherwise, how could those flashy stars have lost the election?

The humorous master Lin Yutang said in his "Analects" that "Yun in 'Six Chapters of a Floating Life' is the most beautiful woman in China." As for Yun's appearance, it was not very beautiful. Her husband Shen Sanbai even said, "Her two teeth are slightly exposed, which is not considered a good appearance." It should be known that Mr. Lin's aesthetic focus is on the charm of language and the elegance of arguments. Yun possesses these two qualities, so we can well imagine her face being lovely, and it is no wonder that Mr. Lin would say that she is the most beautiful woman in China.

Zhang Liying was willing to marry Chen Youren because Zhang called Chen the most beautiful man in the world, and the conditions for beauty are: no whoring, no gambling, no drinking, no smoking, and good health. As for the ages of Zhang and Chen, although they were very much like a father and daughter, in the end, because of Zhang Liying's idealization of aesthetic attitude, they became a couple.

Do the above three examples not prove the recent trend of aesthetic attitude towards idealism? In other words, the materialistic aesthetic attitude, which was once considered immutable, has also changed. This "change" is, of course, progressive and revolutionary.

Fishing and Killing the Family 326

— (Meng)

Fengchun sent the pearl to Ding Yuanwai and said, "This pearl was obtained by my father-in-law while fishing with a net; I am sending it to the Yuanwai to ask for an exemption from the fishing tax!"

Ding Yuanwai took the pearl and said, "Since this pearl was obtained from my lake, it is mine; the fishing tax must still be paid separately!"

Sweet Dream 327

— Jingjia

"… Sweet dream, deep love in the dream, love is strong…"

In the early morning, the alarm clock woke me up, and I lazily lay in bed, unwilling to get up. Spring is a cursed season! It always makes people feel weak!

A low "Sweet Dream" song came from the neighboring room, accompanied by the trembling of the moon guitar, the sound was so sad, making me feel a burst of bitterness on the tip of my nose.

I remembered my dream last night. Yes, there was a lovely dream, a sweet dream, that I had last night. I slept very late last night, and as soon as I fell asleep, I dreamed of the realm I loved. In the dream, I did not win the first prize of the sixth aviation lottery, nor did I make myself become a very powerful official. I only dreamed that I was leaning on the bridge railing of a certain garden, and on the opposite side of the bridge there was a cluster of emerald green trees, in the gaps of the lush branches there was a…

Beautiful girl's face, smiling at me, smiling quietly. The water waves under the bridge also reflected that cluster of trees, that face. We didn't speak, always sitting and smiling at each other, smiling, smiling quietly.

The dream unfolded, and I was no longer leaning on the bridge railing, and the beautiful face between the branches also disappeared. I seemed to be sitting on a huge lawn, with my hands clasped around my knees. There was a bright, round moon in the sky, and I looked at the lovely sky and that bright moon. Suddenly, in that round moon, I saw that sweet smiling face again. Nothing had changed, it was still smiling so quietly… A dark cloud rose up, covering the bright moon, covering that lovely face. The earth was enveloped in darkness… Then I woke up. The clock downstairs was striking four times. If it weren't for the song from the neighboring room, I would have forgotten that I had such a lovely dream last night. However, what's the use of remembering it? I am not in the dream now, that lovely smiling face is neither in the branches nor on the moon!

"… I wish to be in this dream forever…" I was dazed! I seemed to have lost my soul.

New Annotations of Common Sayings 328

— Jianping

A beggar without a stick suffers the wrath of dogs.

Annotation: A dignified country is repeatedly humiliated by Japanese soldiers.

Inserting flowers in a shaved head, enduring pain for the sake of appearance.

Annotation: Puyi claiming the title of emperor, currying favor with the Japanese; appearing glorious on the surface, but suffering in his heart.

A villager recognizes a night pot, a belly full of urine. (Book)

Annotation: Zheng Xiaoxu wrote the declaration of the country.

A villager does not recognize a hunchback, a long back. (Generation)

Annotation: The relationship between the puppet state and Japan. A message child (ear pick) strikes a gong, it does not resonate.

Annotation: The puppet state asks the great powers to recognize it, and the countries ignore it. Robbers litigate, losing every time. Annotation: Our country's diplomacy.

Drawing white powder on the wall, no trace left. Annotation: The disappearance of the China National Aviation Corporation's plane.

Forgetting ancestors when seeing money. Annotation: The madness of traitors.

Playing a show at Huangshi Bridge, regretting it is too late. (Note: Huangshi Bridge is outside Fengmen in Suzhou. It is said that every time a show is performed to repay the gods, it will definitely rain, hence this saying.)

Annotation: Before the execution of the kidnappers, they describe the tragic situation of the family.

Two Views on Love 329

— Ms. Jiong

Since the banner of the women's movement was unfurled, a large group of women who had been oppressed in the deep continent for thousands of years have been able to obtain opportunities for liberation and run to society to enjoy various rights and obligations with men, shattering the feudal traditional thinking inherited for several years. The chains that weighed on women must therefore be gradually broken, and a new bulwark is being built on the future of women!

Although in the past, the union of men and women suffered from the pain of "parents' orders, matchmaker's words," women especially felt that the pain of those unions that had not undergone love was ten thousand times greater than that of men! The ancient teachings of "good horses are not matched with lame saddles, and fierce women do not marry two husbands" state that if a man feels the pain of "parents' orders, matchmaker's words" and is very dissatisfied with his wife, he can arbitrarily vent his sexual desires outside, or marry another wife, and society will not punish him, and he will even think it is an honor. If a woman suffers all kinds of oppression from her husband, and scolding from her in-laws, and feels great pain, she can only succumb to the whipping of etiquette and cannot say a word about divorce or remarriage!…

All the feudal and traditional poisons are gradually drifting away with the tide of the times! Therefore, the unreasonable system of union between men and women according to "parents' orders, matchmaker's words" in the past is now gradually abolished and replaced with a new look.

The union of men and women must go through the process of "love," what a wonderful noun! As a result, young people in general, relying on their own temporary enthusiasm, often run to two extremely different paths - "lovers of love above all else" and "extremists of sexual desire."

The so-called "lovers of love above all else" negate all materialistic theories. They believe that only love can promote their survival in the world. There is no life, no everything, without love. Love is sacred and inviolable, it is supreme. They do not know whether there are hungry people in the world, who do not even talk about love! Many female compatriots who are still trapped under the feudal forces, bound by the "three obediences and four virtues," have no chance to talk about love. Therefore, we must know that love is absolute and is limited by time and space.

Next, let's talk about "extremists of sexual desire." In this week's women's corner in Shenbao, Jun Biyun said it well: "Some new-style young men and women, under the banner of love above all else, believe that the relationship between the sexes is not love, but only 'sexual desire.' So today they vent their sexual desires here, and tomorrow they go there to steal fragrance and jade. This is simply losing reason, and even…

These are crude and simple materialists who simply do not understand what is called 'love'." Based on her words, we admit that she said:

(1) Love is not supreme, but is limited by human life, the times, and society;

(2) Love is not inferior, just a thing to purely vent sexual desire, we have no way to completely deny the emotional role in love;

(3) Love is not only a combination of sex and emotion, but also a combination of life. Our love must be built on the basis of mutual understanding, mutual encouragement, and consistency of thought and action, and in life, we must not forget to work hard to improve human life and promote social work at all times;

Therefore, in the end, all phenomena of my party are rolling around in malformation and morbidity with the current system. If this entire system is not healthy, and the abnormal is used to solve the problems of this part, it is still difficult to be optimistic!

Novel

Tomorrow (8) 330

— Mu Lin

"How sorrowful, this autumn rain,

How sorrowful, I am sick at this time,"

It has been more than ten days since I wrote in my diary. I don't want to record these sad and bitter days of my life. If there is a day to destroy this diary, wouldn't everything be in vain? If it can survive with me, it will only cause my sadness in the future. The past is not worth remembering. Isn't my flower-like life going to be taken away by this autumn wind and autumn rain? I accidentally read a poem without a title in the newspaper, and I especially cherish the first two lines of it, so I wrote it here.

Lately, I have been like a hero going to justice. I enthusiastically helped my mother prepare for the wedding, and it seems that the days are passing too slowly. When the bridal sedan chair is carried out the door, isn't everything over? Why bother waiting until noon three quarters for the execution!

When he came, I also boldly joked and teased him. He advised me to be more stable and not so self-destructive. As long as I understood his heart, he would be grateful to me for the rest of his life. Ah, this poor man!

Today, relatives have all come to my house. This temple-like house suddenly became lively. Moreover, it is right for everyone to laugh with their mouths wide open when doing happy events. Hahaha, let everyone laugh. My mother lost a daughter, but brought back a son-in-law. This profitable business is worth doing for everyone. Congratulations, congratulations, I don't know how many hundreds of times I have heard it. Let me congratulate. Can the people in this world know that the person who is suffering the loss is destroying herself?

I put on a smile to deal with every relative, making their laughter and shouts of congratulations more than worth it. It was all for my sake that they were mobilizing everyone. They would no longer say that I didn't know how to appreciate kindness. This whole house is extremely lively. I should be proud that a girl who is about to be sold is the center of attention for these few days. Of course, the goods decorated in the tree window must be especially careful, so that the big customers can buy them back. Maybe they will be taken out of the dark warehouse and be able to swagger out in a car! As for their survival after going out, no one will think about it.

When he went back yesterday, he gave me a slip of paper, asking me to sneak out to the cinema today to meet him. What is this sneaky business again? I have to agree to him. In the afternoon, I made an excuse to buy leather shoes and took a car straight to the cinema. He was already waiting for me at the door. After buying two tickets for the balcony, we sat like a couple in love.

"What's the matter?" I asked directly.

"I have a few words to say." He replied hesitatingly, that poor man! I held his hand tightly, "Xiong Ge, don't be so miserable, I can agree to everything for you!"

He grasped my hand gratefully. He seemed to have a lot to say, but he kept staring at my face, and finally said, "Do you love me?"

I almost wanted to laugh out loud, nodded, the lights just went out, and I snuggled in his arms. I was satisfied with these two hours of love enjoyment. My soul has been attached to his body, let this body that will rot away in an instant go!

When the show was over, he didn't dare to send me back. After I hired a car, he also left.

Last night, I sat alone at my desk until dawn before going to bed, wanting to write down some of the fantasies at that time, but I couldn't remember anything. Fantasy is not a fact after all!
